1// Take a look at the license at the top of the repository in the LICENSE file.

3use glib::translate::*;
4use glib::GString;
5use libc::c_uint;
6use std::mem;
7
8#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord, Hash)]
9pub struct Key(u32);
10
11impl ::std::ops::Deref for Key {
12    type Target = u32;
13
14    fn deref(&self) -> &u32 {
15        &self.0
16    }
17}
18
19impl ::std::ops::DerefMut for Key {
20    fn deref_mut(&mut self) -> &mut u32 {
21        &mut self.0
22    }
23}
24
25impl ::std::convert::From<u32> for Key {
26    fn from(value: u32) -> Self {
27        skip_assert_initialized!();
28        Self(value)
29    }
30}
31
32impl FromGlib<u32> for Key {
33    unsafe fn from_glib(value: u32) -> Self {
34        skip_assert_initialized!();
35        Self(value)
36    }
37}
38
39impl IntoGlib for Key {
40    type GlibType = u32;
41
42    fn into_glib(self) -> u32 {
43        *self
44    }
45}
46
47impl Key {
48    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_from_name")]
49    pub fn from_name(keyval_name: &str) -> Self {
50        skip_assert_initialized!();
51        Self(unsafe { ffi::gdk_keyval_from_name(keyval_name.to_glib_none().0) })
52    }
53
54    #[doc(alias = "gdk_unicode_to_keyval")]
55    pub fn from_unicode(c: char) -> Self {
56        skip_assert_initialized!();
57        Self(unsafe { ffi::gdk_unicode_to_keyval(u32::from(c)) })
58    }
59
60    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_to_unicode")]
61    pub fn to_unicode(&self) -> Option<char> {
62        skip_assert_initialized!();
63        unsafe { ::std::char::from_u32(ffi::gdk_keyval_to_unicode(**self)).filter(|x| *x != '\0') }
64    }
65
66    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_name")]
67    pub fn name(&self) -> Option<GString> {
68        skip_assert_initialized!();
69        unsafe { from_glib_none(ffi::gdk_keyval_name(**self as c_uint)) }
70    }
71
72    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_is_upper")]
73    pub fn is_upper(&self) -> bool {
74        skip_assert_initialized!();
75        unsafe { from_glib(ffi::gdk_keyval_is_upper(**self)) }
76    }
77
78    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_is_lower")]
79    pub fn is_lower(&self) -> bool {
80        skip_assert_initialized!();
81        unsafe { from_glib(ffi::gdk_keyval_is_lower(**self)) }
82    }
83
84    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_to_upper")]
85    #[must_use]
86    pub fn to_upper(&self) -> Self {
87        skip_assert_initialized!();
88        unsafe { ffi::gdk_keyval_to_upper(**self) }.into()
89    }
90
91    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_to_lower")]
92    #[must_use]
93    pub fn to_lower(&self) -> Self {
94        skip_assert_initialized!();
95        unsafe { ffi::gdk_keyval_to_lower(**self) }.into()
96    }
97
98    #[doc(alias = "gdk_keyval_convert_case")]
99    pub fn convert_case(&self) -> (Self, Self) {
100        skip_assert_initialized!();
101        unsafe {
102            let mut lower = mem::MaybeUninit::uninit();
103            let mut upper = mem::MaybeUninit::uninit();
104            ffi::gdk_keyval_convert_case(self.0, lower.as_mut_ptr(), upper.as_mut_ptr());
105            let lower = lower.assume_init();
106            let upper = upper.assume_init();
107            (Self(lower), Self(upper))
108        }
109    }
110}
111
112impl ::std::fmt::Display for Key {
113    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> ::std::fmt::Result {
114        write!(f, "Key({})", self.0)
115    }
116}
117
